! Verbs
!
! Negative verbs
! Copula
! Main verbs


LEXICON Negativeverb

ii+V+Neg:0 negmood ;

LEXICON negmood
+Ind:0 negind ;
+Imp:0 negimp ;
+Sup:0 negsup ;

LEXICON negind
+Sg1:in K ;
+Sg2:it K ;
+Sg3:ii K ;
+Du1:ean K ;
+Du2:eahppi K ;
+Du3:eaba K ;
+Pl1:eat K ;
+Pl2:ehpet K ;
+Pl3:eai K ;

LEXICON negimp
+Sg1:allon K ;
+Sg2:ale K ;
+Sg3:allos K ;
+Du1:al'lu K ;
+Du2:al'li K ;
+Du3:alloska K ;
+Pl1:allot K ;
+Pl2:allet K ;
+Pl3:alloset K ;

LEXICON negsup
+Sg1:aman K ;
+Sg2:amat K ;
+Sg3:amai K ;
+Du1:amame K ;
+Du2:amade K ;
+Du3:amaska K ;
+Pl1:amamet K ;
+Pl2:amadet K ;
+Pl3:amaset K ;


LEXICON Copula ! Dividing into finite and infinite
leat+V:l Finitecop ;
leat+V:l Infinitecop ;

LEXICON Finitecop
+Ind+Prs:0 Prscop ;
+Ind+Prs+ConNeg:eat K ;
+Ind+Prt:0 Prtcop ;
+Cond+Prs:ivc1c1e CondC ; ! regular cond, pointer to 3syll paradigm
+Cond+Prs:ivc1c1o PrtV ;  ! alternate cond, pointer to 2syll par
+Cond+Prs+Sg3:ivc1c1e K ; ! special cond for Sg3
+Pot+Prs+Sg3:eas1 K ;    ! all Pot pointers copied from sme-lex
+Pot+Prs+Sg3:es1 K ;
+Pot+Prs+ConNeg:eas1 K ;
+Pot+Prs+ConNeg:es1 K ;
+Pot+Prs:eaz1z1a PrsV ;
+Imprt+Prs:0 Impcop ;
+Imprt+Prs+ConNeg:eage K ;
+Imprt+Prs+ConNegII:ehko K ;

LEXICON Prscop
+Sg1:ean K ;
+Sg2:eat K ;
+Sg3:ea K ;
+Du1:etne K ;
+Du1:edne K ;
+Du2:eahppi K ;
+Du3:eaba K ;
+Pl1:eat K ;
+Pl2:ehpet K ;
+Pl3:eat K ;

LEXICON Prtcop
+Sg1:edjen K ;
+Sg2:edjet K ;
+Sg3:ej K ;
+Sg3:eaj K ;
+Du1:ejmme K ;
+Du2:ejdde K ;
+Du3:ejgga K ;
+Du3:eajgga K ;
+Pl1:ejmmet K ;
+Pl2:ejddet K ;
+Pl3:edje K ;

LEXICON Impcop
+Sg1:ehkon K ;
+Sg2:eage K ;
+Sg3:ehkos K ;
+Sg3:eaj K ;
+Du1:eadnu K ;
+Du1:eahkku K ;
+Du2:eahkki K ;
+Du3:ehkoska K ;
+Pl1:ehkot K ;
+Pl:eatnot K ;
+Pl2:ehket K ;
+Pl3:ehkoset K ;

LEXICON Infinitecop
+Inf:eahkit K ;
+Inf:eat K ;
+Act:eahkin K ;
+Act+Ess:eamen K ;
+Act+Ess:eame K ;
+Act+Ess:eahkime K ;
+Act+Loc:eames K ;
+PrfPrc:ean K ;
+PrfPrc:eamas1 K ;

LEXICON VerbRoot
